kwaɓazalwane isiǁuku saɓantu esasikʰona ndawoɲe kwakuŋatʰi ikʰulu namaʃumi amaɓili watʰi madoda ɓazalwane kwakumelwe ukuɓa kuɡǀ̤waliseke umbhalo umoja oŋǀ̤wele awukʰulumajo ŋapʰambili ŋomlomo kadavide ŋod͡ʒuda owajeŋumholi kulaɓo aɓaɓamba ud͡ʒesu ŋokuɓa wajeɓalwe kaɲe natʰi watʰola isaɓelo kule ŋkonzo lowoke wazuza insimu ŋomvuzo wokuŋaluŋi wawa ŋekʰanda waǃʰuma pʰakatʰi neziɓilini zakʰe zoŋke zaǀʰitʰeka kwaziwa jiɓo ɓoŋke aɓakʰilejo ed͡ʒerusalema jaze jaǃaɲd͡ʒwa lejo nsimu ŋolimi lwakuɓo ŋokutʰi iakeldama okuŋukutʰi insimu jeɡazi ŋokuɓa kulot͡ʃiwe eŋǀwadini jamahuɓo ukutʰi umuzi wakʰe mawuɓe jiɬane kuŋaɓikʰo oɬala kuwo nokutʰi isikʰunɮa sakʰe asitʰatʰwe ŋomuɲe ŋakʰo kulawo madoda ajehamba natʰi isikʰatʰi soŋke lapʰo iŋkosi ud͡ʒesu iŋena ipʰuma pʰakatʰi kwetʰu kuǃalela embhapatʰizweni kad͡ʒohane kwaze kwaɓa lusuku akʰuʃulwa ŋalo kitʰi kumelwe ukuɓa eɲe kuwo iɓe ŋufakazi kaɲe natʰi ŋokuvuka kwakʰe ɓase ɓemisa aɓaɓili ud͡ʒosefa otʰiwa uɓarsaɓa otʰiwa futʰi ud͡ʒustu kaɲe nomatʰija ɓase ɓekʰuleka ɓetʰi wena ŋkosi owazi izinɬizijo zaɓantu ɓoŋke ake ukʰombe omuɲe kulaɓa aɓaɓili omkʰetʰilejo ukuɓa atʰatʰe isikʰunɮa sale ŋkonzo noɓupʰostoli apʰambuka kuso ud͡ʒuda ukuja endaweni jakʰe ɓase ɓeɓenzela iŋkatʰo jaɮa umatʰija waɓalwa kaɲe naɓapʰostoli aɓajiʃumi naɲe kwatʰi sekufikile usuku lwepʰentekoste ɓoŋke ɓaɓeɓutʰene ndawoɲe ŋokuŋazelelwe kwavela ezulwini inɬokomo kwaŋatʰi ejokuvuŋuza komoja onamanɮa jona jaɡǀ̤walisa inɮu joŋke aɓaɓeɬezi kujo kwase kuɓonakala kuɓo izilimi ezaɬukenejo kuŋatʰi ezomlilo zaɬala pʰezu kwalowo nalowo kuɓo ɓase ɓeɡǀ̤wala ɓoŋke umoja oŋǀ̤wele ɓaǃala ukukʰuluma ŋeziɲe izilimi ɲd͡ʒeŋalokʰo umoja waɓapʰa ukupʰumisela kepʰa kwakukʰona aɓad͡ʒuda aɓakʰile ed͡ʒerusalema amadoda akʰolwajo evela ezizweni zoŋke ezipʰansi kwezulu kwatʰi kuzwakele lowo mdumo uǃuǃaɓa lwaɓutʰana lwapʰitʰiza ŋokuɓa kwaɓa jilowo nalowo waɓezwa ɓekʰuluma ŋolimi lwakuɓo ɓetʰuka ɓamaŋala ɓatʰi beka ɓoŋke laɓa aɓakʰulumajo aɓasiɓo aɓaseɡalile na jini pʰo ukuɓa soŋke ŋaɓaɲe sizwe ŋolimi lwakitʰi esazalwa nalo na amaparte namamede namaelamitʰi naɓakʰile emesopotamija nased͡ʒudija nasekʰapʰadosija nasepontu naseasija nasefriɡija nasepʰamfilija naseɡiɓitʰe nasezweni laseliɓija ŋasekʰurene nezihambi zaseroma naɓad͡ʒuda namaproselite aɓasekretʰe naɓasearaɓija sijaɓezwa ɓekʰuluma ŋezilimi zakitʰi ŋemiseɓenzi emikʰulu kaŋkuluŋkulu ɓoŋke ɓamaŋala ɓasambatʰeka ɓatʰi omuɲe komuɲe kutʰini lokʰu na kepʰa aɓaɲe ɓeɓabuǃa ɓatʰi ɓaɡǀ̤wele iwajini elimnandi wajesesukuma upetru naɓajiʃumi naɲe wapʰakamisa izwi lakʰe wapʰumisela watʰi kuɓo madoda akwad͡ʒuda nani noŋke enakʰilejo ed͡ʒerusalema makwazeke lokʰu kini niɓeke inɮeɓe emazwini ami ŋokuɓa laɓa kaɓadakiwe ɲd͡ʒeŋokuǀaɓaŋa kwenu lokʰu kusejihora lesitʰatʰu lemini kodwa lokʰu kujikʰo okwakʰuluɲwa ŋomprofetʰi ud͡ʒoweli ukutʰi ‘kujakutʰi ezinsukwini zokupʰela kuʃo uŋkuluŋkulu ŋijakutʰulula umoja wami pʰezu kwajo joŋke iɲama amadodana enu namadodakazi enu ajakuprofetʰa izinsizwa zenu ziɓone imiɓono aɓadala ɓenu ɓapʰupʰe amapʰupʰo jeɓo napʰezu kweziŋǀeku zami neziŋǀekukazi zami ŋijakutʰulula umoja wami ŋalejo miɬa zijakuprofetʰa ŋijakuveza izimaŋaliso ezulwini pʰezulu neziɓonakaliso emɬaɓeni pʰansi iɡazi nomlilo nokutʰuŋǃa komusi ilaŋa lijakupʰenduka uɓumɲama iɲaŋa iɓe jiɡazi luŋakafiki usuku olukʰulu noluǃʰamilejo lweŋkosi kujakutʰi jilowo nalowo oɓiza iɡama leŋkosi ujakusindiswa madoda akwaisrajeli zwanini lawa mazwi ud͡ʒesu wasenazaretʰa indoda efakazelwe ŋuŋkuluŋkulu pʰambi kwenu ŋemiseɓenzi jamanɮa naŋezimaŋaliso naŋeziɓonakaliso uŋkuluŋkulu azenza ŋaje pʰakatʰi kwenu ɲd͡ʒeŋalokʰu nazi nina uǃoɓo lwenu jena lo esenikelwe ŋesu elimisiwejo naŋokwazipʰambili kukaŋkuluŋkulu nambetʰela ŋezanɮa zaɓaŋenamtʰetʰo nambulala lowo uŋkuluŋkulu wamvusa etʰukulula imiɲd͡ʒuɲd͡ʒu jokufa lokʰu kwakuŋenakwenzeka ukuɓa aɓaɲd͡ʒwe jikʰo ŋokuɓa udavide utʰi ŋaje ‘ŋajiɓona iŋkosi pʰambi kwami ɲd͡ʒalo ŋokuɓa iŋakwesokunene sami ukuze ŋiŋaɲakaziswa ŋalokʰo inɬizijo jami ijad͡ʒaɓula nolimi lwami lujetʰaɓa ŋiʃo neɲama jami ijakuɬala ŋokwetʰemba ŋokuɓa awujikuʃija umpʰefumulo wami ehajidese futʰi awujikuvuma oŋǀ̤wele wakʰo aɓone ukuɓola waŋazisa izinɮela zokupʰila ujakuŋiɡǀ̤walisa ŋokud͡ʒaɓula eɓusweni ɓakʰo madoda ɓazalwane ake ŋikʰulume kini ŋokusoɓala ŋokʰokʰo udavide ukutʰi wafa nokutʰi wembelwa nokutʰi itʰuna lakʰe lisekʰona kitʰi nanamuɬa ŋakʰo lokʰu eŋumprofetʰi ekwazi ukutʰi uŋkuluŋkulu wajefuŋile kuje ŋesifuŋo ukutʰi enzalweni jokʰalo lwakʰe ujakuɓeka omuɲe esiɬalweni sakʰe soɓukʰosi eɓona kuse pʰambili wakʰuluma ŋokuvuka kukakristu ukutʰi akaʃijwaŋa ehajidese neɲama jakʰe ajiɓonaŋa ukuɓola ud͡ʒesu lo uŋkuluŋkulu wamvusa esiŋofakazi ɓakʰo tʰina soŋke ŋakʰo epʰakaɲiselwe ŋakwesokunene sikaŋkuluŋkulu esamukele kujise isitʰembiso sikamoja oŋǀ̤wele wakutʰulula lokʰu enikuɓonajo nenikuzwajo ŋokuɓa udavide akeɲukelaŋa ezulwini kepʰa jena utʰi ‘iŋkosi jatʰi eŋkosini jami ɬala ŋakwesokunene sami ŋize ŋiɓeke izitʰa zakʰo ziɓe jisenaɓelo seziɲawo zakʰo ŋakʰo inɮu joŋke jakwaisrajeli majazi impela ukutʰi uŋkuluŋkulu umenzile iŋkosi nokristu ud͡ʒesu lo enambetʰela nina esipʰambanweni seɓekuzwa ɓaɬaɓeka enɬizijweni ɓatʰi kupetru nakwaɓaɲe aɓapʰostoli madoda ɓazalwane sijakwenze ɲd͡ʒani na upetru wajesetʰi pʰendukani jilowo nalowo abapatʰizwe eɡameni likad͡ʒesu kristu kukʰo ukutʰetʰelelwa kwezono zenu kʰona nijakwamukeliswa isipʰiwo sikamoja oŋǀ̤wele ŋokuɓa isitʰembiso ŋesenu nesaɓantwana ɓenu esaɓo ɓoŋke aɓakude ɓoŋke iŋkosi uŋkuluŋkulu wetʰu ejakuɓaɓiza wafakaza naŋamaɲe amazwi amaniŋi waɓajala watʰi zisindiseni kulesi sizukulwane esipʰambenejo ŋakʰo aɓalamukelejo izwi lakʰe ɓabapatʰizwa kwenezelwa ŋalowo muɬa aɓantu kuŋatʰi iziŋkuluŋwane ezintatʰu ɓaǃinisela ɲd͡ʒalo esifundisweni saɓapʰostoli nasekuɬaŋaneni nasekuɬepʰuleni isiŋkwa nasemikʰulekweni kepʰa kwaɓa jilowo nalowo muntu weɬelwa ŋukwesaɓa kwenziwa ŋaɓapʰostoli izimaŋaliso neziɓonakaliso eziniŋi ɓoŋke aɓakʰolwajo ɓaɓe ndawoɲe ɓaɬaŋaɲela izinto zoŋke ɓatʰeŋisa ŋemfujo naŋempaɬa ɓaɓela ɓoŋke ŋajo ɲd͡ʒeŋokuswela kwaɓo imiɬa ŋemiɬa ɓaǃinisela ŋanɬizijoɲe etʰempelini ɓaɬepʰula isiŋkwa ekʰaja ɓaɮa ukuɮa kwaɓo ŋentokozo naŋoɓumɬopʰe ɓenɬizijo ɓemdumisa uŋkuluŋkulu ɓetʰandeka kuɓantu ɓoŋke iŋkosi jenezela eɓanɮeni imiɬa ŋemiɬa aɓasindiswajo upetru nod͡ʒohane ɓakʰupʰukela etʰempelini ŋehora lokukʰuleka elesiʃijaɡaloluɲe kwase kuletʰwa indoda etʰile ejisiʃoʃa kwasesiswini sikanina aɓaɓejiɓeka imiɬa ŋemiɬa ŋasemɲaŋo wetʰempeli otʰiwa omuɬe ukuɓa iǀele ukwaɓelwa izipʰo kwaɓaŋenajo etʰempelini kwatʰi ukuɓa aɓone opetru nod͡ʒohane ɓezakuŋena etʰempelini waǀela ukwaɓelwa isipʰo kepʰa upetru wamɡǃ̤olozela kaɲe nod͡ʒohane watʰi sibeke wajeseɓabeka etʰemba ukuɓa amukele utʰo kuɓo kodwa upetru watʰi isiliva neɡolide aŋinalo kepʰa lokʰo eŋinakʰo ŋikupʰa kʰona eɡameni likad͡ʒesu kristu wasenazaretʰa hamba wajesembamba ŋesanɮa sokunene wamsukumisa kwaǃina masiɲane iziɲawo zakʰe namaǃakala eɡǁ̤uma wema wahamba waŋena naɓo etʰempelini ehamba eɡǁ̤uma emdumisa uŋkuluŋkulu aɓantu ɓoŋke ɓambona ehamba edumisa uŋkuluŋkulu kepʰa ɓase ɓemazi ukuɓa ŋujena owajeɬalela ukupʰiwa ŋasemɲaŋo omuɬe wetʰempeli ɓeɬelwa ŋukwesaɓa nokumaŋala ŋokwenzakele kuje esaɓambelele kopetru nod͡ʒohane ɓoŋke aɓantu ɓaɡid͡ʒimela kuɓo empʰemeni otʰiwa okasolomoni ɓesaɓa kakʰulu kʰona upetru eɓona lokʰo watʰatʰa watʰi kuɓantu madoda akwaisrajeli nimaŋalelani ŋalona nisiɡǃ̤olozelelani ŋokuŋatʰi simenze ukuɓa ahambe ŋawetʰu amanɮa naŋokwetʰu ukukʰolwa na uŋkuluŋkulu kaaɓrahama nokaisaka nokad͡ʒakoɓe uŋkuluŋkulu wawoɓaɓa ɓetʰu ujidumisile iŋǀeku jakʰe ud͡ʒesu enajikʰapʰela najipʰika eɓusweni ɓukapilatu jena eseŋǃumile ukujikʰulula kepʰa nina nampʰika oŋǀ̤wele noluŋilejo naǀela ukuɓa nipʰiwe oŋumbulali najiɓulala iŋkosi jokupʰila ajivusajo uŋkuluŋkulu kwaɓafilejo esiŋofakazi ɓakʰo tʰina ŋokukʰolwa eɡameni lajo lo enimbonajo nenimazijo iɡama lajo lamenza aǃine nokukʰolwa okuŋajo kumnike le mpilo pʰambi kwenu noŋke kalokʰu ɓazalwane ŋijazi ukutʰi nenza lokʰo ŋokuŋazi ɲd͡ʒeŋaɓo aɓaɓusi ɓenu kepʰa lokʰo uŋkuluŋkulu akumemezela ŋapʰambili ŋomlomo waɓaprofetʰi ɓoŋke ukutʰi ukristu wakʰe ujakuɬupʰeka ukuɡǀ̤walisile kaɲd͡ʒe ŋalokʰu pʰendukani niɡuǃuke ukuɓa kuɬaŋulwe izono zenu ukuze kufike izikʰatʰi zokuɬuɲelelwa ezivela eɓusweni ɓeŋkosi nokuɓa itʰume ukristu d͡ʒesu enimmiselwejo okumelwe ukuɓa izulu limamukele kuze kuɓe jizikʰatʰi zokuɓujiselwa kwakʰo koŋke uŋkuluŋkulu akʰuluma ŋakʰo ŋomlomo waɓaprofetʰi ɓakʰe aɓaŋǀ̤wele kusukela kwapʰakade umose kambe watʰi ‘iŋkosi uŋkuluŋkulu ijakunivusela umprofetʰi kuɓazalwane ɓenu ɲd͡ʒeŋami nijakumlalela kukʰo koŋke azakukukʰuluma kini kujakutʰi woŋke umuntu oŋajikumlalela lowo mprofetʰi ujakuǀʰitʰwa kuɓantu jeɓo naɓaprofetʰi ɓoŋke kusukela kusamuweli naɓalandelajo ɓoŋke aɓakʰulumilejo ɓamemezela lezo zinsuku nina niŋamadodana aɓaprofetʰi nawesivumelwano uŋkuluŋkulu asenzajo nawojiɬo etʰi kuaɓrahama ‘ŋenzalo jakʰo ijakuɓusiswa imindeni joŋke jomɬaɓa uŋkuluŋkulu esejivusile iŋǀeku jakʰe wajitʰumela kini kuǃala ukuniɓusisa ŋokuniɡuǃula kuɓe jilowo nalowo kini eɓuɓini ɓakʰe kepʰa ɓesakʰuluma kuɓantu aɓapristi nenduna jetʰempeli naɓasadusi ɓaɓafikela ɓeneŋwa ŋukufundisa kwaɓo aɓantu nokumemezela ŋod͡ʒesu ukuvuka kwaɓafilejo ɓaɓaɓamba ɓaɓafaka etiloŋweni kwaze kwaɓa kusasa ŋokuɓa kwase kuɬwile kepʰa aɓaniŋi kwaɓezwajo izwi ɓakʰolwa umumo wamadoda waɓa kuŋatʰi iziŋkuluŋwane ezijisiɬanu kwatʰi ŋaŋomuso kwaɓutʰana ed͡ʒerusalema aɓaɓusi namaluŋa naɓabali ɓaɓo noanase umpristi omkʰulu nokajafase nod͡ʒohane noaleksandru naɓo ɓoŋke aɓenɮu jompristi omkʰulu ɓaɓamisa pʰakatʰi kwaɓo ɓaɓaɓuza ɓatʰi lokʰo nikwenze ŋamapʰi amanɮa naŋalipʰi iɡama na kʰona upetru eɡǀ̤wele umoja oŋǀ̤wele watʰi kuɓo nina ɓaɓusi ɓezizwe namaluŋa ŋǁa siɓuzwa namuɬa ŋomseɓenzi omuɬe kumuntu oɡulajo ukutʰi jena usindiswe ŋani makwazeke kini noŋke nasesizweni soŋke sakwaisrajeli ukutʰi ŋeɡama likad͡ʒesu kristu wasenazaretʰa enambetʰela esipʰambanweni amvusajo uŋkuluŋkulu kwaɓafilejo ŋaje umi lo muntu pʰambi kwenu esindile jena ujit͡ʃe eladelelwa jinina ɓakʰi eselaɓa jinɬoko jeɡumbi ajikʰo insindiso ŋomuɲe ŋokuɓa alikʰo futʰi eliɲe iɡama pʰansi kwezulu elinikiwe eɓantwini esimelwe ukusindiswa ŋalo kwatʰi ɓeɓona isiɓindi sikapetru nod͡ʒohane ɓeǃonda ukutʰi ɓaŋaɓantu aɓaŋafundile ɓajimifunda ɲd͡ʒe ɓamaŋala ɓaɓazi ukutʰi kade ɓenod͡ʒesu kepʰa ɓeɓona umuntu opʰilisiwejo emi naɓo ɓaɓeŋenakupʰika lutʰo kodwa seɓeɓajalile ukuɓa ɓapʰume empʰakatʰini ɓalulekana ɓodwa ɓatʰi sizakuɓenzani laɓa ɓantu na ŋokuɓa kusoɓala kuɓo ɓoŋke aɓakʰilejo ed͡ʒerusalema ukutʰi isiɓonakaliso esiǃʰamilejo senziwe jiɓo asinakukupʰika kodwa ukuze kuŋaɓe kusanda pʰakatʰi kwaɓantu asiɓalaje ɓaŋaɓe ɓesakʰuluma kumuntu namuɲe ŋalelo ɡama ɓase ɓeɓaɓiza ɓaɓajala ŋokutʰi ɓaŋakʰulumi ɓaŋafundisi nakaɲe ŋeɡama likad͡ʒesu kepʰa opetru nod͡ʒohane ɓapʰendula ɓatʰi kuɓo ŋǃumani nina ukuɓa kuluŋile jini eɓusweni ɓukaŋkuluŋkulu ukulalela nina kunoŋkuluŋkulu ŋokuɓa tʰina asinakujeka ukukʰuluma ŋalokʰo esikuɓonilejo nesikuzwilejo kʰona seɓeɓalajile futʰi ɓaɓajeka ɓeŋafumanaŋa ukutʰi ɓaŋaɓad͡ʒezisa kaɲd͡ʒani ŋeŋǁa jaɓantu ŋokuɓa ɓoŋke ɓedumisa uŋkuluŋkulu ŋalokʰo okwenzekilejo ŋokuɓa umuntu esenziwe kuje leso siɓonakaliso sokupʰulukiswa wajenemiɲaka eve emaʃumini amane seɓejekiwe ɓaja kwaɓakuɓo ɓaɓika koŋke aɓapristi aɓakʰulu namaluŋa aɓekuʃilo kuɓo ɓona seɓezwile ɓapʰakamisa izwi kuŋkuluŋkulu ŋanɬizijoɲe ɓatʰi somanɮa wena owenza izulu nomɬaɓa nolwanɮe nakʰo koŋke okukukʰo owaʃo ŋomoja oŋǀ̤wele ŋomlomo kaɓaɓa udavide iŋǀeku jakʰo ukutʰi ‘kuŋani ukuɓa aɓezizwe ɓaǁokozele naɓantu ɓaǀeɓe okujize na amakʰosi omɬaɓa aǃʰelile naɓaɓusi ɓajiɬaŋaɲele iŋkosi noɡǀ̤ot͡ʃiwejo wajo ŋokuɓa ŋempela oherode nopontiju pilatu kaɲe naɓezizwe naɓantu ɓakwaisrajeli ɓajiɬaŋaɲela kulo muzi iŋǀeku jakʰo eŋǀ̤wele ud͡ʒesu owamɡǀ̤oɓajo ukuzakukwenza lokʰo okumiswe ŋapʰambili jisanɮa neǀeɓo lakʰo ukuɓa kwenzeke maɲd͡ʒeke ŋkosi beka ukusoŋela kwaɓo unike iziŋǀeku zakʰo ukuɓa zikʰulume izwi lakʰo ŋaso soŋke isiɓindi ŋokwelula isanɮa sakʰo ukupʰulukisa kwenziwe iziɓonakaliso nezimaŋaliso ŋeɡama leŋǀeku jakʰo eŋǀ̤wele ud͡ʒesu kwatʰi seɓekʰulekile kwazaɲazaɲiswa indawo lapʰo ɓeɓeɓutʰene kʰona ɓaɡǀ̤waliswa ɓoŋke ŋumoja oŋǀ̤wele ɓakʰuluma izwi likaŋkuluŋkulu ŋesiɓindi isiǁuku saɓakʰolwajo sasinɬizijoɲe nompʰefumulo muɲe akwaɓakʰo nojedwa owaʃo ŋezimpaɬa zakʰe ukutʰi ŋezakʰe kodwa ɓakuɬaŋaɲela koŋke aɓapʰostoli ɓaveza ŋamanɮa amakʰulu uɓufakazi ŋokuvuka kweŋkosi ud͡ʒesu umusa omkʰulu wawupʰezu kwaɓo ɓoŋke kwakuŋekʰo oswelajo pʰakatʰi kwaɓo ŋokuɓa ɓoŋke aɓaɓeŋaɓanikazi ɓamazwe noma ɓezinɮu ɓatʰeŋisa ŋakʰo ɓaletʰa imali jalokʰo aɓatʰeŋise ŋakʰo ɓajiɓeka ŋaseziɲaweni zaɓapʰostoli kwaɓa jilowo nalowo waɓelwa ɲd͡ʒeŋokuswela kwakʰe kwatʰi ud͡ʒosefa owatʰiwa ŋaɓapʰostoli uɓarnaɓa okuŋukutʰi ŋokuhuɲuʃwa indodana jenduduzo umlevi wasekʰupro ŋokuzalwa enensimu watʰeŋisa ŋajo waletʰa imali wajiɓeka ŋaseziɲaweni zaɓapʰostoli kepʰa indoda etʰile iɡama lajo liŋuananija inosafira umkajo jatʰeŋisa ŋendawo jaɡoɮa iŋǁeɲe jemali nomkajo ekwazi jaletʰa iŋǁeɲe etʰile jajiɓeka ŋaseziɲaweni zaɓapʰostoli wajesetʰi upetru ananija kuŋani ukuɓa usatʰane aɡǀ̤walise inɬizijo jakʰo uǃambe amaŋa kumoja oŋǀ̤wele uɡoɮe iŋǁeɲe jemali jezwe na lisekʰona ɓeliŋesilo elakʰo na selitʰeŋisiwe ɓeliŋekʰo emanɮeni akʰo na ujiɓekeleni lejo nto enɬizijweni jakʰo na awuǃambaŋa amaŋa kuɓantu kepʰa kuŋkuluŋkulu kutʰe uananija ezwa lawo mazwi wawa pʰansi wafa ukwesaɓa okukʰulu kweɬela ɓoŋke aɓezwa lokʰo izinsizwa zasuka zamsoŋelezela zamkʰipʰela pʰanɮe zammbela kwatʰi emva kwesikʰatʰi esiŋaɓa ŋamahora amatʰatʰu kwaŋena nomkakʰe eŋakwazi okwenzakelejo upetru wajesetʰatʰa etʰi ŋit͡ʃele ukuɓa izwe nilitʰeŋise ŋokuŋaka na watʰi jeɓo ŋokuŋaka kepʰa upetru watʰi kuje kuŋani ukuɓa nivumelene ŋokuliŋa umoja weŋkosi na beka iziɲawo zaɓambele indoda jakʰo zisemɲaŋo nawe ɓazakukukʰipʰela pʰanɮe wajesewa pʰansi masiɲane ŋaseziɲaweni zakʰe wafa izinsizwa zaŋena zamfumana efile zamkʰipʰela pʰanɮe zammbela ŋasendodeni jakʰe ukwesaɓa okukʰulu kwaleɬela iɓanɮa loŋke naɓo ɓoŋke aɓezwa lokʰo kwenziwa izimaŋaliso neziɓonakaliso eziniŋi eɓantwini ŋezanɮa zaɓapʰostoli ɓoŋke ɓaɓe nɬizijoɲe ɓesempʰemeni kasolomoni kepʰa kwaɓaɲe akwaɓakʰo owajenesiɓindi sokuziɬaŋanisa naɓo kepʰa aɓantu ɓaɓeɓazisa kakʰulu ɓenezelwa kakʰulu aɓakʰolwa jiŋkosi aɓaniŋi naɓesilisa naɓesifazane ŋaŋokuɓa ɓakʰipʰela pʰanɮe emiɡwaǃweni aɓaɡulajo ɓaɓaɓeka emaǀansini nasezinɬakeni kuze kutʰi lapʰo eza upetru isitʰunzi ɲd͡ʒe sakʰe sisitʰiɓeze aɓaɲe kuɓo kwaɓutʰana nesiǁuku esivela emizini ezuŋeze id͡ʒerusalema ɓeletʰa aɓaɡulajo naɓakʰatʰazwa ŋawomoja aɓaŋǀ̤olilejo ɓapʰulukiswa ɓoŋke kwase kusuka umpristi omkʰulu naɓo ɓoŋke aɓaɓe naje aɓaŋaɓeɬelo laɓasadusi ɓaɡǀ̤wala umhawu ɓaɓamba aɓapʰostoli ɓaɓafaka etiloŋweni lombuso kepʰa iŋelosi jeŋkosi javula imiɲaŋo jetiloŋo eɓusuku jaɓakʰipʰa jatʰi hambani nime nikʰulume etʰempelini kuɓantu amazwi oŋke alokʰu kupʰila kwatʰi seɓezwile ɓaŋena etʰempelini ekutʰatʰeni kokusa ɓafundisa kepʰa kwafika umpristi omkʰulu naɓaɓe naje ɓaɓizela ndawoɲe umpʰakatʰi neziɡele zoŋke zaɓantwana ɓakwaisrajeli ɓatʰumela enɮini jeziɓoʃwa ukuɓa ɓaletʰwe kepʰa izikʰonzi ezafika kʰona aziɓafumanaŋa etiloŋweni zase ziɓujela emuva zaɓika zatʰi inɮu jeziɓoʃwa sajifumana ivaliwe iǃinile impela naɓalindi ɓemi emiɲaŋo kepʰa sesivulile asifumanaŋa muntu ŋapʰakatʰi kwatʰi ukuɓa induna jetʰempeli naɓapristi aɓakʰulu ɓezwe lawo mazwi ɓasambatʰeka ŋawo ŋokutʰi kuŋaɓa jini lokʰo na kepʰa kwafika omuɲe waɓaɓikela watʰi bekani amadoda eɓeniwafakile etiloŋweni emi etʰempelini afundisa aɓantu kʰona japʰuma induna kaɲe nezikʰonzi zaɓaletʰa kuŋeŋampoǃo ŋokuɓa ɓeɓesaɓa aɓantu funa ɓakʰandwe ŋamat͡ʃe seɓeɓaletʰile ɓaɓamisa empʰakatʰini umpristi omkʰulu waɓaɓuza watʰi sanijala nokunijala ukuɓa niŋafundisi ŋalelo ɡama bekani seniɡǀ̤walise id͡ʒerusalema ŋesifundiso senu niɬose ukweɬisela iɡazi lalowo muntu pʰezu kwetʰu kepʰa upetru naɓapʰostoli ɓapʰendula ɓatʰi simelwe ukulalela uŋkuluŋkulu kunaɓantu uŋkuluŋkulu wawoɓaɓa wamvusa ud͡ʒesu enambulala nina ŋokumpʰaɲeka emtʰini lowo uŋkuluŋkulu wampʰakamisa ŋesokunene sakʰe aɓe jiŋkosi nomsindisi ukuɓa anike uisrajeli ukupʰenduka nokutʰetʰelelwa kwezono tʰina siŋofakazi ɓalezo zinto kaɲe nomoja oŋǀ̤wele uŋkuluŋkulu amnikile laɓo aɓamlalelajo ɓona seɓezwile ɓatʰukutʰela ɓafuna ukuɓaɓulala kwase kusukuma omuɲe empʰakatʰini umfarisi oɡama lakʰe liŋuɡamalijeli isazimtʰetʰo esitusekajo esizweni soŋke wajala ukuɓa aɓantu ɓakʰiʃwe isikʰaʃana wajesetʰi kuɓo madoda akwaisrajeli ǃapʰelani kulokʰo enizakukwenza kulaɓa ɓantu ŋokuɓa ŋapʰambi kwalezi zinsuku kwasuka utʰewuda eziʃaja omkʰulu kwanamatʰela kuje amadoda aŋatʰi amakʰulu amane waɓulawa jena naɓo ɓoŋke aɓamlalelajo ɓaǀʰitʰeka ɓapʰela emva kwalowo kwasuka ud͡ʒuda waseɡalile ezinsukwini zokubalwa waɬuɓukisa aɓantu ukuɓa ɓamlandele nalowo wabuba naɓo ɓoŋke aɓamlalelajo ɓaɬakazeka maɲd͡ʒeke ŋitʰi kini dedani kulaɓa ɓantu niɓajeke ŋokuɓa uma leli su nalo mseɓenzi kuvela kuɓantu kujakuǀʰitʰeka kepʰa uma kuvela kuŋkuluŋkulu anijikuɓa namanɮa okuɓaǀʰitʰa funa mɬawumbe nifuɲanwe niŋaɓalwajo noŋkuluŋkulu ɓamvumelake ɓase ɓeɓaɓiza aɓapʰostoli ɓaɓaʃaja ɓaɓajala ŋokutʰi ɓaŋakʰulumi ŋeɡama likad͡ʒesu ɓaɓakʰulula kʰona ɓasuka pʰambi kompʰakatʰi ɓetʰokoza ŋokuɓa ɓeɓefanele ukuduɲazwa ŋeŋǁa jalelo ɡama aɓajekaŋa ukufundisa nokuʃumajela ivaŋeli ŋod͡ʒesu kristu imiɬa joŋke etʰempelini nasemakʰaja kwatʰi ŋalejo miɬa aɓafundi seɓanda kwavela ukukʰonona kuɓad͡ʒuda aɓakʰuluma isiɡreki ŋamaheɓeru ŋokutʰi aɓafelokazi ɓakuɓo ɓajaŋǀiʃwa ekwaɓelweni kwemiɬa ŋemiɬa aɓajiʃumi nambili ɓase ɓeɓiza iɓanɮa laɓafundi ɓatʰi akukuɬe ukuɓa tʰina siʃije izwi likaŋkuluŋkulu sikʰonze ematafuleni funanike pʰakatʰi kwenu ɓazalwane amadoda ajisikʰombisa anodumo oluɬe aɡǀ̤wele umoja nokuɬakanipʰa esiŋawamisela lowo mseɓenzi kepʰa tʰina sizakuǃinisela ekukʰulekeni naseŋkonzweni jezwi leli zwi laɓa liɬe kulo loŋke iɓanɮa ɓase ɓekʰetʰa ustefanu umuntu owajeɡǀ̤wele ukukʰolwa nomoja oŋǀ̤wele nofilipʰu noprokʰoro nonikanori notʰimoni nopʰarmena nonikolawu iproselite laseantijokija ɓaɓamisa pʰambi kwaɓapʰostoli ɓakʰuleka ɓaɓeka izanɮa pʰezu kwaɓo izwi likaŋkuluŋkulu landa umumo waɓafundi wakʰula ed͡ʒerusalema nesiǁuku esikʰulu saɓapristi salalela iŋkolo kepʰa ustefanu eɡǀ̤wele umusa namanɮa wenza izimaŋaliso neziɓonakaliso eziŋkulu pʰakatʰi kwaɓantu kwase kusuka aɓaɲe ɓesinaɡoɡe elitʰiwa elaɓaliɓertino naɓasekʰurene naɓasealeksandrija naɓavela ekʰilikʰija naseasija ɓapʰikisana nostefanu kepʰa ɓaɓeŋenamanɮa okumelana nokuɬakanipʰa nomoja ajekʰuluma ŋakʰo kʰona ɓatʰeŋa amadoda atʰi simzwile ekʰuluma amazwi enɬamba ŋomose naŋoŋkuluŋkulu ɓavusa aɓantu namaluŋa naɓabali ɓamvukela ɓambamba ɓamjisa empʰakatʰini ɓamisa ofakazi ɓamaŋa aɓatʰi lo muntu akajeki ukukʰuluma amazwi ŋale ndawo eŋǀ̤wele naŋomtʰetʰo ŋokuɓa simzwile etʰi ud͡ʒesu lo wasenazaretʰa uzakuǀʰitʰa le ndawo aɡuǃule imitʰetʰo asinika jona umose kwatʰi ɓemɡǃ̤olozela ɓoŋke aɓaɓeɬezi empʰakatʰini ɓaɓona uɓuso ɓakʰe kuŋatʰi uɓuso ɓeŋelosi umpristi omkʰulu wajesetʰi nembala lokʰu kuɲd͡ʒalo na jena watʰi madoda ɓazalwane nani ɓoɓaɓa lalelani uŋkuluŋkulu weŋkazimulo waɓonakala kuɓaɓa uaɓrahama esemesopotamija eŋakakʰi eharana watʰi kuje ‘pʰuma ezweni lakini naseziɬot͡ʃeni zakʰo uje ezweni eŋizakukukʰombisa lona kʰona wapʰuma ezweni lamakaledi waja wakʰa eharana kwatʰi esefile ujise uŋkuluŋkulu wamsusa lapʰo wamɬalisa kuleli zwe enakʰe kulo nina maɲd͡ʒe kepʰa akamnikaŋa ifa kulo ŋiʃo neliŋaŋoɲawo watʰembisa kodwa ukutʰi uzakumnika lona liɓe ŋelakʰe nelenzalo jakʰe emva kwakʰe eŋakaɓi namntwana uŋkuluŋkulu wakʰuluma kaɲd͡ʒe watʰi ‘inzalo jakʰe izakuɓa ŋumfokazi ezweni lezizwe ɓajakujenza iziɡǃ̤ila ɓajipʰatʰe kaɓi imiɲaka eŋamakʰulu amane kepʰa leso sizwe aɓajakuɓa jiziɡǃ̤ila kuso ŋijakusaɬulela mina waʃo uŋkuluŋkulu andukuɓa ɓapʰume ɓaŋikʰonze kule ndawo wajesemnika isivumelwano sokusoka kaɲd͡ʒaloke wazala uisaka wamsoka ŋosuku lwesiʃijaɡalombili uisaka wazala ud͡ʒakoɓe ud͡ʒakoɓe wazala okʰokʰo aɓajiʃumi nambili okʰokʰo ɓaɓa nomhawu ŋod͡ʒosefa ɓatʰeŋisa ŋaje wasiwa eɡiɓitʰe kodwa uŋkuluŋkulu wajenaje wamkʰipʰa kuzo zoŋke izinɬupʰeko zakʰe wamupʰa umusa nokuɬakanipʰa pʰambi kukafaro iŋkosi jaseɡiɓitʰe jena wammisa aɓe ŋumbusi eɡiɓitʰe nakujo joŋke inɮu jakʰe kepʰa kwafika inɮala kulo loŋke iɡiɓitʰe nakwakʰanani nokuɬupʰeka okukʰulu oɓaɓa kaɓafumana ukuɮa ud͡ʒakoɓe esezwile ukutʰi kukʰona ukuɮa eɡiɓitʰe watʰuma oɓaɓa ŋokokuǃala kwatʰi ŋokwesiɓili ud͡ʒosefa waziwa ŋaɓafowaɓo kwaɓonakala kufaro isizwe sakuɓo kad͡ʒosefa ud͡ʒosefa wajesetʰumela waɓiza ud͡ʒakoɓe ujise naɓakuɓo ɓoŋke aɓantu aɓaŋamaʃumi ajisikʰombisa nanɬanu ud͡ʒakoɓe weɬela eɡiɓitʰe wafa jena nawoɓaɓa ɓajiswa esikemi ɓaɓekwa etʰuneni alitʰeŋa uaɓrahama ŋenani lesiliva kumadodana kahamori esikemi kepʰa sesisondele isikʰatʰi sesitʰembiso uŋkuluŋkulu asiʃo kuaɓrahama ɓanda aɓantu ɓaɓa ɓaniŋi eɡiɓitʰe kwaze kwavela eɲe iŋkosi eɡiɓitʰe eɓiŋamazi ud͡ʒosefa jona jasipʰatʰa ŋoɓuǃili isizwe sakitʰi jaɓaɬupʰa oɓaɓa ŋokuɓalaɬisa iziŋane zaɓo ziŋapʰili ŋaleso sikʰatʰi kwazalwa umose waɓa muɬe kuŋkuluŋkulu wonɮiwa iziɲaŋa ezintatʰu enɮini kajise eselaɬiwe indodakazi kafaro jamtʰola jazonɮela jena ukuɓa aɓe jindodana jajo umose wafundiswa ukuɬakanipʰa koŋke kwaɓaseɡiɓitʰe waɓa namanɮa ŋamazwi naŋemiseɓenzi jakʰe kutʰe esenemiɲaka eŋamaʃumi amane ezelwe kwafika enɬizijweni jakʰe ukuɓa aɓamele aɓafowaɓo aɓantwana ɓakwaisrajeli waɓona umuntu epʰatʰwa kaɓi wamvikela wampʰindisela oɬuʃwajo wambulala owaseɡiɓitʰe uɓetʰemba ukutʰi aɓafowaɓo ɓajakuǃonda ukutʰi uŋkuluŋkulu uɓanika ukusindiswa ŋesanɮa sakʰe kepʰa aɓakuǃondaŋa naŋaŋomuso wafika kuɓo ɓelwa wazama ukuɓalamula ɓaɓujisane watʰi ‘madoda niŋaɓazalwane nipʰatʰanelani kaɓi na kepʰa lowo owajemona umakʰelwane wakʰe wamɬoɬoloza watʰi ‘uɓekwe ŋuɓani uɓe ŋumbusi nomaɬuleli pʰezu kwetʰu na usufuna ukuŋiɓulala nami ɲd͡ʒeŋalokʰo uɓulele owaseɡiɓitʰe izolo na kʰona umose waɓaleka ŋeŋǁa jalelo zwi waɓa ŋumfokazi ezweni lakwamidijani lapʰo azala kʰona amadodana amaɓili kwatʰi sekupʰelele imiɲaka eŋamaʃumi amane kwaɓonakala kuje eɬane lentaɓa jasesinaji iŋelosi iselaŋaɓini lomlilo esiɬaɬeni umose ekuɓona wamaŋala ŋalowo mbono esasondela ukuɓa abekisise kwafika izwi leŋkosi latʰi ‘ŋiŋuŋkuluŋkulu wawojiɬo uŋkuluŋkulu kaaɓrahama nokaisaka nokad͡ʒakoɓe umose watʰutʰumela akaɓa nasiɓindi sokubekisisa iŋkosi jajisitʰi kuje ‘kʰumula iziǀatʰulo eziɲaweni zakʰo ŋokuɓa indawo omi kujo iŋumɬaɓatʰi oŋǀ̤wele ŋikuɓonile nokukuɓona ukuɬuʃwa kwesizwe sami esiseɡiɓitʰe ŋizwile ukuɓuɓula kwaso seŋeɬile ukuɓa ŋiɓakʰipʰe woza kalokʰu ŋizakukutʰumela eɡiɓitʰe umose lowo aɓamalajo ɓetʰi ‘uɓekwe ŋuɓani uɓe ŋumbusi nomaɬuleli na ŋujena amtʰumajo uŋkuluŋkulu ŋesanɮa seŋelosi ejaɓonakala kuje esiɬaɬeni aɓe ŋumbusi nomɬeŋi jena lowo waɓakʰipʰa enza izimaŋaliso neziɓonakaliso ezweni laseɡiɓitʰe naselwanɮe oluɓomvu naseɬane imiɲaka eŋamaʃumi amane ŋuje umose lowo owatʰi kuɓantwana ɓakwaisrajeli ‘uŋkuluŋkulu ujakunivusela umprofetʰi kuɓafowenu oɲd͡ʒeŋami ŋuje lowo owajeseɓanɮeni eɬane kaɲe neŋelosi ejakʰuluma naje entaɓeni jasesinaji kaɲe nawoɓaɓa nowamukela amazwi okupʰila ukuze aninike wona kepʰa oɓaɓa aɓavumaŋa ukumlalela kodwa ɓamɬoɬoloza ɓaɓujela emuva eɡiɓitʰe ŋezinɬizijo zaɓo ɓatʰi kuaroni ‘senzele oŋkuluŋkulu aɓazakuhamba pʰambi kwetʰu ŋokuɓa umose lowo owasikʰipʰa ezweni laseɡiɓitʰe asazi ukuɓa weɬelwe jini ɓenza itʰole ŋalejo miɬa ɓaletʰa umɬat͡ʃelo esitʰombeni ɓad͡ʒaɓula ŋemiseɓenzi jezanɮa zaɓo kepʰa uŋkuluŋkulu waɓafulatʰela waɓadedela ukuɓa ɓakʰonze iɓanɮa lezulu ɲd͡ʒeŋokuɓa kulot͡ʃiwe eŋǀwadini jaɓaprofetʰi ukutʰi ‘naniŋiletʰela iminikelo nemiɬat͡ʃelo imiɲaka eŋamaʃumi amane eɬane nina nɮu kaisrajeli na ǃʰa natʰatʰa itende likamoloki neŋkaɲezi kaŋkuluŋkulu uremfani imifanekiso enajenza ukuɓa nikʰuleke kujo ŋijakunimukisela ŋapʰambili kweɓaɓiloni kwakukʰona itende loɓufakazi koɓaɓa eɬane ɲd͡ʒeŋalokʰo akujalajo jena owakʰuluma nomose ukuɓa alenze ŋomfanekiso aɓewuɓonile oɓaɓa ɓenod͡ʒoʃuwa ɓalamukela ɓaliŋenisa ezweni lezizwe aziǁoʃajo uŋkuluŋkulu eɓusweni ɓawoɓaɓa kwaze kwaɓa semiɬeni kadavide owatʰola umusa eɓusweni ɓukaŋkuluŋkulu waǀela ukufunela uŋkuluŋkulu kad͡ʒakoɓe idokodo kepʰa ŋusolomoni owamakʰela inɮu kodwa opʰezukoŋke akaɬali ezinɮini ezenziwe ŋezanɮa ɲd͡ʒeŋokuʃo komprofetʰi ukutʰi ‘izulu lijisiɬalo sami soɓukʰosi nomɬaɓa ujisenaɓelo seziɲawo zami ŋeɲd͡ʒani inɮu enijakuŋakʰela jona iʃo iŋkosi ‘noma jijipʰi indawo jami jokupʰumula na isanɮa sami asikwenzaŋa koŋke lokʰo na nina ɓantamo zilukʰuni aɓaŋasokile ezinɬizijweni nasezinɮeɓeni nimelana ɲd͡ʒalo nomoja oŋǀ̤wele ɲd͡ʒeŋojiɬo niɲd͡ʒalo nani ŋumupʰi kuɓaprofetʰi ojiɬo aɓaŋamziŋelaŋa na ɓaɓaɓulala aɓaɓememezela ŋapʰambili ukuza koluŋilejo eseniŋaɓakʰapʰeli naɓaɓulali ɓakʰe nina enamukela umtʰetʰo ŋokujala kweziŋelosi kepʰa aniwuɡǀ̤inaŋa kwatʰi ɓekuzwa lokʰo ɓaɬaɓeka ezinɬizijweni ɓamɡuɡudela amaziɲo kepʰa jena eɡǀ̤wele umoja oŋǀ̤wele waɡǃ̤olozela ezulwini waɓona iŋkazimulo kaŋkuluŋkulu nod͡ʒesu emi ŋakwesokunene sikaŋkuluŋkulu watʰi beka ŋiɓona izulu livuliwe nendodana jomuntu imi ŋakwesokunene sikaŋkuluŋkulu ɓase ɓekʰamuluka ŋezwi elikʰulu ɓavala izinɮeɓe ɓatʰeleka kuje kaɲekaɲe ɓamkʰipʰela ŋapʰanɮe komuzi ɓamkʰanda ŋamat͡ʃe ofakazi ɓaɓeka iziŋuɓo zaɓo ŋaseziɲaweni zensizwa eɡama lajo liŋusawulu ustefanu ɓamkʰanda ŋamat͡ʃe ekʰuleka etʰi ŋkosi d͡ʒesu jamukela umoja wami wajeseɡuǃa pʰansi wamemeza ŋezwi elikʰulu watʰi ŋkosi uŋaɓaɓaleli lesi sono eseʃilo lokʰo walala uɓutʰoŋo kepʰa usawulu wajevumelene naɓo ŋokuɓulawa kwakʰe ŋalolo suku kwavela ukuziŋelwa okukʰulu kweɓanɮa lased͡ʒerusalema ɓaɬakazeka ɓoŋke emazweni ased͡ʒudija nasesamarija kwasala aɓapʰostoli ɓodwa amadoda akʰolwajo ammbela ustefanu amkʰalela isililo esikʰulu kepʰa usawulu waliǀʰitʰa iɓanɮa eŋena ezinɮini ŋezinɮu ehudula aɓesilisa naɓesifazane waɓafaka etiloŋweni aɓaɬakazekilejo ɓase ɓehamba ɓeʃumajela izwi levaŋeli ufilipʰu weɬela emzini wasesamarija waɓaʃumajeza ukristu iziǁuku zalalela ŋanɬizijoɲe okwakʰuluɲwa ŋufilipʰu zizwa ziɓona iziɓonakaliso azenzajo ŋokuɓa kwapʰuma omoja aɓaŋǀ̤olilejo kwaɓaniŋi aɓakʰwelwa jiɓo ɓememeza ŋezwi elikʰulu naɓaniŋi aɓafe uɬaŋotʰi naɓajiziɲoŋa ɓapʰulukiswa kwaɓa kʰona ukutʰokoza okukʰulu kulowo muzi kepʰa kwakukʰona indoda etʰile ŋusimoni iɡama lajo ejajikade jenza imiliŋo kulowo muzi isimaŋalisa isizwe sasesamarija iziʃaja umuntu omkʰulu ɓanamatʰela kuje ɓoŋke kusukela kwaɓaŋǀiɲane kuze kuɓe kwaɓakʰulu ɓetʰi lo uŋamanɮa kaŋkuluŋkulu aɓizwa ŋokutʰi makʰulu ɓaɓenamatʰela kuje ŋokuɓa eɓamaŋalisile isikʰatʰi eside ŋemiliŋo jakʰe kepʰa ɓatʰi ukuɓa ɓakʰolwe ŋufilipʰu eʃumajela ivaŋeli ŋombuso kaŋkuluŋkulu naŋeɡama likad͡ʒesu kristu ɓabapatʰizwa aɓesilisa naɓesifazane naje usimoni wakʰolwa watʰi esebapatʰiziwe wanamatʰela kufilipʰu wamaŋala eɓona iziɓonakaliso nemiseɓenzi emikʰulu jamanɮa ejenziwajo kwatʰi ukuɓa aɓapʰostoli ɓased͡ʒerusalema ɓezwe ukutʰi isamarija lilamukele izwi likaŋkuluŋkulu ɓatʰumela kuɓo opetru nod͡ʒohane seɓeɬele kʰona ɓaɓakʰulekela ukuɓa ɓamukele umoja oŋǀ̤wele ŋokuɓa wajeŋakeɬeli nakojedwa kuɓo kodwa ɓaɓesabapatʰiziwe eɡameni leŋkosi ud͡ʒesu kupʰela kʰona ɓaɓeka izanɮa pʰezu kwaɓo ɓase ɓamukelake umoja oŋǀ̤wele kepʰa usimoni eɓonile ukutʰi ŋokuɓekwa kwezanɮa zaɓapʰostoli ujapʰiwa umoja waletʰa imali kuɓo watʰi ŋipʰeni nami lawo manɮa ukuze jilowo nalowo eŋiɓeka izanɮa pʰezu kwakʰe amukele umoja oŋǀ̤wele kepʰa upetru watʰi kuje isiliva lakʰo malibube kaɲe nawe ŋokuɓa utʰi isipʰo sikaŋkuluŋkulu siŋatʰeŋwa ŋemali awunasaɓelo nalifa kuleli zwi ŋokuɓa inɬizijo jakʰo ajiluŋile pʰambi kukaŋkuluŋkulu ŋakʰoke pʰenduka kuloɓu ɓuɓi ɓakʰo uŋǁuse eŋkosini iŋaɓe uŋatʰetʰelelwa jini isizinɮo senɬizijo jakʰo ŋokuɓa ŋijaɓona ukutʰi useɲoŋweni eɓaɓajo nasekuɓoʃweni kokuɓi usimoni wajesepʰendula etʰi ŋiŋǁuseleni nina eŋkosini ukuze kuŋeɬeli lutʰo kimi lwalokʰo enikuʃilojo kutʰe seɓefakazile ɓelikʰulumile izwi leŋkosi ɓaɓujela ed͡ʒerusalema ɓaʃumajela ivaŋeli emizaneni eminiŋi jaɓasesamarija kepʰa iŋelosi jeŋkosi jakʰuluma kufilipʰu jatʰi suka uje ŋaseniŋizimu enɮeleni epʰuma ed͡ʒerusalema eɬela eɡaza jona ijiɬane wajesesuka wahamba beka nansi indoda jaseetijopija umtʰenwa isikʰulu sikakʰandakʰe iŋkosikazi jaseetijopija eɓipʰezu kweŋǀ̤eɓo jajo joŋke eɓifikile ed͡ʒerusalema izakukʰuleka iɓisiɓuja iɬezi eŋǃoleni jajo ifunda umprofetʰi uisaja umoja watʰi kufilipʰu sondela unamatʰele kulejo ŋǃola ufilipʰu wajeseɡid͡ʒimela kujo wajizwa ifunda umprofetʰi uisaja watʰi ujakuǃonda kambe lokʰu okufundajo na jona jatʰi ŋiŋakwazi kaɲd͡ʒani uma kuŋekʰo oŋiholajo na jamŋǁusa ufilipʰu ukuɓa akʰwele aɬale najo kepʰa isaɬukwana sombhalo eɓisifunda jilesi esitʰi wajiswa ekuɬat͡ʃweni ɲd͡ʒeŋemvu ɲd͡ʒeŋewunɮu elitʰule pʰambi komɡundi walo kaɲd͡ʒalo kawuvulaŋa umlomo wakʰe ekutʰoɓeleni kwakʰe ukwaɬulelwa kwakʰe kwasuswa ŋuɓani oŋalanda ŋesizukulwane sakʰe na ŋokuɓa ukupʰila kwakʰe kujasuswa emɬaɓeni kepʰa umtʰenwa watʰatʰa watʰi kufilipʰu ŋijaǀela umprofetʰi ukʰuluma lokʰo ŋoɓani na uziʃo jena noma omuɲe na ufilipʰu wavula umlomo joŋke kuŋenziwa wapʰendula watʰi ŋijakʰolwa ukutʰi ud͡ʒesu kristu ujindodana kaŋkuluŋkulu wajala ukuɓa iŋǃola ime ɓeɬela emanzini ɓoɓaɓili ufilipʰu nomtʰenwa wambhapatʰiza kwatʰi seɓekʰupʰukile kepʰa usawulu esafutʰa ŋokusoŋela nokuɓulala aɓafundi ɓeŋkosi waja kumpristi omkʰulu waǀela kuje iziŋǀwadi zokuja edamaseku emasinaɡoɡeni kuze kutʰi uma efumana aɓantu ɓalejo nɮela aɓesilisa naɓesifazane aɓajise ed͡ʒerusalema ɓeɓoʃiwe kepʰa ekuhambeni kwakʰe esesondela edamaseku kwambaneka masiɲane ŋǁazoŋke ukukʰaɲa okuvela ezulwini wawa pʰansi emɬaɓatʰini wezwa izwi litʰi kuje sawulu sawulu uŋiziŋelelani na kulukʰuni kuwe ukukʰaɬela eziŋkandini wajesetʰi uŋuɓani ŋkosi jatʰi mina ŋiŋud͡ʒesu omziŋelajo wena kodwa vuka uŋene emzini uzakut͡ʃelwa lokʰu omelwe ukukwenza kepʰa amadoda ajehamba naje ajemi eŋenakukʰuluma ŋokuɓa ezwa izwi kodwa ajeŋaɓoni muntu usawulu wajesevuka pʰansi kepʰa esevulile ameɬo akʰe kaɓonaŋa lutʰo ɓase ɓembamba ŋesanɮa ɓamjisa edamaseku izinsuku zaɓa siǃondile ufune enɮini kad͡ʒuda umuntu oɡama lakʰe liŋusawulu wasetarsu ŋokuɓa beka ujakʰuleka uɓonile indoda iɡama lajo liŋuananija iŋena iɓeka izanɮa pʰezu kwakʰe ukuɓa aɓone kepʰa uananija wapʰendula watʰi ŋkosi ŋizwile ŋaɓaniŋi ŋalejo ndoda koŋke okuɓi ekwenzile kwaɓaŋǀ̤wele ɓakʰo ed͡ʒerusalema nalapʰa unamanɮa avela kuɓapristi aɓakʰulu okuɓopʰa ɓoŋke aɓakʰuleka eɡameni lakʰo iŋkosi jajisitʰi kuje hamba ŋokuɓa lo ujisit͡ʃa sami esikʰetʰiwejo sokupʰatʰa iɡama lami pʰambi kwaɓezizwe namakʰosi naɓantwana ɓakwaisrajeli ŋokuɓa mina ŋizakumbonisa koŋke amelwe ukuɬuʃwa ŋakʰo ŋeŋǁa jeɡama lami kʰona wahamba uananija waŋena enɮini waɓeka izanɮa pʰezu kwakʰe watʰi sawulu umzalwane iŋkosi ud͡ʒesu ejaɓonakala kuwe enɮeleni oze ŋajo iŋitʰumile ukuɓa uɓuje uɓone uɡǀ̤waliswe ŋomoja udorka ŋokuhuɲuʃwa jena wajenemiseɓenzi eminiŋi emiɬe nokwaɓela aɓampofu izipʰo kwatʰi ŋalezo zinsuku waɡula wafa seɓemɡezile ɓambeka ekamelweni elipʰezulu kepʰa ilida laliseduze ned͡ʒopʰa ŋakʰoke aɓafundi seɓezwile ukutʰi upetru ukʰona lapʰo ɓatʰuma kuje amadoda amaɓili emŋǀeŋa etʰi uŋaliɓali ukuza kitʰi wajesesuka upetru wahamba naɓo esefikile ɓamjisa ekamelweni elipʰezulu aɓafelokazi ɓoŋke ɓeza kuje ɓekʰala ɓembonisa izambatʰo neziŋuɓo aɓezenzile udorka esenaɓo kepʰa upetru waɓakʰipʰa ɓoŋke waɡuǃa ŋamadolo wakʰuleka wapʰendukela esiduɲd͡ʒini watʰi tʰaɓitʰa vuka wajesevula ameɬo akʰe izinsuku eziniŋi ed͡ʒopʰa kwasimoni umʃuki kwakukʰona ekesarija indoda etʰile eɡama lajo liŋukorneliju ejinduna jekʰulu jeɓutʰo elitʰiwa elaseitalija wajeŋumuntu okʰolwajo nowesaɓa uŋkuluŋkulu kaɲe nenɮu jakʰe joŋke aɓela aɓantu aɓampofu izipʰo eziniŋi ekʰuleka kuŋkuluŋkulu ɲd͡ʒaloɲd͡ʒalo waɓona ŋokusoɓala embonweni iŋelosi kaŋkuluŋkulu iŋena kuje kuŋatʰi ŋehora lesiʃijaɡaloluɲe lemini itʰi korneliju wajiɡǃ̤olozela enokwesaɓa watʰi kwenze ɲd͡ʒani ŋkosi jatʰi kuje imikʰuleko jakʰo nokwaɓela kwakʰo aɓampofu izipʰo kweɲukile kwaɓa jisikʰumbuzo emeɬweni kaŋkuluŋkulu tʰumake amadoda ed͡ʒopʰa uɓize usimoni otʰile otʰiwa upetru jena uŋenisile kwasimoni otʰile umʃuki onɮu jakʰe iŋaselwanɮe isimukile iŋelosi eɓikʰuluma naje waɓiza aɓaɓili ɓenɮu jakʰe neɓutʰo elikʰolwajo kulawo ajeɬala naje ɲd͡ʒalo waɓalandisa koŋke waɓatʰumela ed͡ʒopʰa ŋaŋomuso ɓesahamba laɓo seɓesondela emzini upetru weɲukela pʰezu kwenɮu ukujokʰuleka ŋehora lesitʰupʰa kʰona walamba kakʰulu wafuna ukuɮa kepʰa ɓesamluŋisela weɬelwa jisijezi waɓona izulu livulekile nesit͡ʃa esitʰile seɬa siɲd͡ʒeŋendwaŋu eŋkulu seɬiselwa emɬaɓeni ŋamaǀʰopʰo amane kusona kwakukʰona zoŋke izilwane ezineziɲawo ezine nezinwaɓuzelajo zomɬaɓa neziɲoni zezulu kwavela izwi latʰi kuje vuka petru ɬaɓa uɮe kepʰa upetru watʰi ǃʰa ŋkosi ŋokuɓa aŋizaŋe ŋikuɮe okujiǀʰilo nokuŋǀ̤olilejo izwi lapʰinda laʃo kuje ŋokwesiɓili latʰi lokʰo akuɬambululile uŋkuluŋkulu uŋaʃo wena ukutʰi kuɓi lokʰo kwapʰindwa katʰatʰu isit͡ʃa seɲuselwa masiɲane ezulwini upetru esasambatʰekile ŋokutʰi ŋakuɓe ujini lowo mbono awuɓonilejo beka amadoda ajetʰuɲiwe ŋukorneliju eseɓuzile inɮu kasimoni ema ŋasesaŋweni amemeza eɓuza ukutʰi usimoni otʰiwa upetru uŋenisile jini lapʰo upetru esazinɮa ŋombono umoja watʰi kuje beka amadoda amaɓili ajakufuna sukumake weɬe uhambe naɓo uŋaŋaɓazi ŋalutʰo ŋokuɓa jimina eŋiɓatʰumilejo upetru wajeseɬela kuwo amadoda watʰi bekani jimina enimfunajo kujindaɓani enize ŋajo na ɓatʰi ukorneliju induna wasuka wahamba naɓo aɓatʰile ɓaɓazalwane ɓased͡ʒopʰa ɓampʰelekezela ŋaŋomuso ɓaŋena ekesarija ukorneliju wajeɓalindele eseɓizile iziɬoɓo naɓaŋane ɓakʰe aɓakʰulu kwatʰi ukuɓa aŋene upetru ukorneliju wamɬaŋaɓeza wawa pʰansi ŋaseziɲaweni zakʰe wakʰuleka kepʰa upetru wamvusa watʰi sukuma nami ŋiŋumuntu ɲd͡ʒe esakʰuluma naje waŋena wafumana aɓaniŋi aɓaɓeɓutʰene wajesetʰi nijazi ukutʰi akuvuɲelwe nasekʰupro naseantijokija ɓeŋalikʰulumi izwi kojedwa kuɓad͡ʒuda kupʰela kodwa kwakukʰona aɓaɲe kuɓo amadoda asekʰupro nasekʰurene aɓatʰi ɓefika eantijokija ɓakʰuluma nakumaɡreki ɓeʃumajela ivaŋeli indoda etʰile ejisanusi nomprofetʰi wamaŋa umd͡ʒuda oɡama lakʰe liŋuɓard͡ʒesu owajekʰona kumbusi wezwe userɡiju pawulu umuntu oneŋǃ̤ondo enɬe jena waɓiza oɓarnaɓa nosawulu wafuna ukuzwa izwi likaŋkuluŋkulu kodwa ueluma isanusi ŋokuɓa liɲd͡ʒalo iɡama lakʰe ŋokuhuɲuʃwa wamelana naɓo wafuna ukupʰambukisa umbusi ekukʰolweni kepʰa usawulu osetʰiwa upawulu eɡǀ̤wele umoja oŋǀ̤wele wamɡǃ̤olozela watʰi o wena oɡǀ̤wele iŋkoɬiso joŋke noɓuɓi ɓoŋke ndodana kasatʰane sitʰa sokuluŋa koŋke awujikujeka ukuzipʰambukisa izinɮela eziǃondilejo zeŋkosi na beka isanɮa seŋkosi sipʰezu kwakʰo maɲd͡ʒe uzakuɓa jimpumputʰe kuɓe jisikʰatʰi uŋaliɓoni ilaŋa kwase kumfikela kʰona lapʰo ukufipʰala noɓumɲama wahamba efuna aɓazakumhola ŋesanɮa kʰona umbusi eseɓona okwenzekilejo wakʰolwa emaŋaliswa ŋesifundiso seŋkosi upawulu naɓaɓe naje ɓamuka epʰafu ŋomkʰumbi ɓafika epʰerɡe lasepʰamfilija kepʰa ud͡ʒohane waɬukana naɓo waɓujela ed͡ʒerusalema ɓona ekumukeni kwaɓo epʰerɡe ɓaja eantijokija lasepʰisidija ɓaŋena esinaɡoɡeni ŋosuku lwesaɓatʰa ɓaɬala pʰansi sekufundiwe umtʰetʰo naɓaprofetʰi aɓapʰatʰi ɓesinaɡoɡe ɓatʰumela kuɓo ɓatʰi madoda ɓazalwane uma ninezwi lokujala aɓantu kʰulumani wajesesukuma upawulu waǃʰweɓa ŋesanɮa watʰi madoda akwaisrajeli nani enesaɓa uŋkuluŋkulu lalelani uŋkuluŋkulu walesi sizwe sakwaisrajeli waɓakʰetʰa oɓaɓa waɓapʰakamisa aɓantu ɓeŋaɓafokazi ezweni laseɡiɓitʰe waɓakʰipʰa kulo ŋeŋalo epʰakemejo waɓaɓekezelela eɬane kuŋatʰi imiɲaka eŋamaʃumi amane waǀʰitʰa izizwe ezijisikʰombisa ezweni lasekʰanani waɓaɓela izwe lazo liɓe jifa kwaɮula kuŋatʰi imiɲaka eŋamakʰulu amane namaʃumi ajisiɬanu emva kwalokʰo waɓanika aɓaɬuleli kwaze kwaɓa ŋusamuweli umprofetʰi kusukela lapʰo ɓaǀela iŋkosi uŋkuluŋkulu waɓanika usawule indodana kakisi umuntu wesizwe sakwaɓeɲd͡ʒamini imiɲaka eŋamaʃumi amane esemkʰipʰile waɓavusela udavide aɓe jiŋkosi afakaza ŋaje ukutʰi ‘ŋimfumene udavide kad͡ʒesaji umuntu oŋowenɬizijo jami ojakwenza koŋke eŋikutʰandajo enzalweni jakʰe uŋkuluŋkulu waletʰela uisrajeli umsindisi ud͡ʒesu ɲd͡ʒeŋokwetʰembisa kwakʰe eŋakafiki jena ud͡ʒohane wajeseʃumajele kuso soŋke isizwe sakwaisrajeli umbhapatʰizo wokupʰenduka eseɡǀ̤ina ukuhamba kwakʰe ud͡ʒohane watʰi ‘lokʰu enitʰi ŋijikʰo aŋisikʰo mina kodwa bekani ujeza emva kwami eŋiŋafanele ukukʰumula isiǀatʰulo seziɲawo zakʰe madoda ɓazalwane madodana oɬaŋa lukaaɓrahama naɓapʰakatʰi kwenu aɓamesaɓajo uŋkuluŋkulu izwi lale nsindiso litʰuɲelwe kitʰi ŋokuɓa aɓakʰilejo ed͡ʒerusalema naɓaɓusi ɓaɓo aɓamazaŋa jena namazwi aɓaprofetʰi afundwa amasaɓatʰa ŋamasaɓatʰa ɓawaɡǀ̤walisa ŋokumlaɬa nakuɓa ɓeŋafumanaŋa iǀala lokufa kuje nokʰo ɓaǀela kupilatu ukuɓa aɓulawe kwatʰi seɓefeze koŋke okwakulot͡ʃiwe ŋaje ɓameɬisa emtʰini ɓambeka etʰuneni kepʰa uŋkuluŋkulu wamvusa kwaɓafilejo waɓonwa izinsuku eziniŋi jiɓo aɓaɓekʰupʰukele naje ed͡ʒerusalema ɓevela eɡalile aseɓeŋofakazi ɓakʰe kuɓantu maɲd͡ʒe natʰi siniʃumajeza ivaŋeli lesitʰembiso esenziwa koɓaɓa ukutʰi uŋkuluŋkulu usiɡǀ̤walisile sona kuɓantwana ɓetʰu ŋokumvusa ud͡ʒesu ɲd͡ʒeŋokuɓa kulot͡ʃiwe futʰi kulo ihuɓo lesiɓili ukutʰi ‘wena ujindodana jami namuɬa ŋikuzele maǃondana nokumvusa kwakʰe kwaɓafilejo ukuɓa eŋasajikuɓujela ekuɓoleni wakʰuluma kaɲd͡ʒe watʰi ‘ŋizakuninika okuŋǀ̤wele nokutʰembekilejo kukadavide ŋakʰo nakweɲe indawo utʰi ‘awujikunika oŋǀ̤wele wakʰo aɓone ukuɓola ŋokuɓa udavide esekʰonzile iǀeɓo likaŋkuluŋkulu esizukulwaneni sakʰe walala uɓutʰoŋo waɓekwa kojise waɓona ukuɓola kepʰa jena amvusajo uŋkuluŋkulu akakuɓonaŋa ukuɓola ŋakʰoke makwazeke kini madoda ɓazalwane ukutʰi ŋalowo kumeɲezelwa kini ukutʰetʰelelwa kwezono nakukʰo koŋke eɓeniŋenakuluŋisiswa kukʰo ŋomtʰetʰo kamose jilowo nalowo okʰolwajo ujakuluŋisiswa ŋaje ŋakʰo ǃapʰelani funa neɬelwe ŋokwakʰuluɲwa ŋaɓaprofetʰi ukutʰi ‘bekani nina zideleli nimaŋale niɲamalale ŋokuɓa mina ŋiseɓenza umseɓenzi emiɬeni jenu umseɓenzi eniŋajikukʰolwa jiwo nakuɓa umuntu enilandisa ŋawo kwatʰi ekupʰumeni kwaɓo ɓaɓaǀela ukuɓa lawo mazwi akʰuluɲwe kuɓo naŋesaɓatʰa elizajo kʰona seɓeɬakazekile aɓesinaɡoɡe aɓaniŋi ɓaɓad͡ʒuda namaproselite aǃotʰo ɓalandela opawulu noɓarnaɓa aɓakʰuluma naɓo ɓeɓaŋǀeŋa ukuɓa ɓaɬale emseni kaŋkuluŋkulu ŋesaɓatʰa elilandelajo kwaɓutʰana kuǀiʃe umuzi woŋke ukuzwa izwi likaŋkuluŋkulu kepʰa aɓad͡ʒuda ɓeɓona iziǁuku ɓaɡǀ̤wala umhawu ɓakupʰika okwakukʰuluɲwa ŋupawulu ɓeɬambalaza kʰona opawulu noɓarnaɓa ɓakʰuluma ŋesiɓindi ɓatʰi ɓekudiŋeka ukuɓa izwi likaŋkuluŋkulu likʰuluɲwe kini kuǃala kepʰa lokʰu niliŋǃaɓa niziʃo nina nitʰi anifanele ukupʰila okupʰakade bekani sesipʰendukela kwaɓezizwe ŋokuɓa iŋkosi isijalezile kaɲd͡ʒalo ukutʰi ‘ŋikuɓekile uɓe ŋukukʰaɲa kwaɓezizwe uɓe jinsindiso kuze kuɓe semkʰawulweni womɬaɓa kwatʰi aɓezizwe ɓekuzwa lokʰo ɓatʰokoza ɓalidumisa izwi leŋkosi ɓakʰolwa ɓoŋke aɓaɓemiselwe ukupʰila okupʰakade izwi leŋkosi lahaɲd͡ʒiswa kulo izwe loŋke kepʰa aɓad͡ʒuda ɓavusa aɓesifazane aɓaǃotʰo aɓanesitʰunzi nezikʰulu zomuzi ɓavusela opawulu noɓarnaɓa ukuziŋelwa ɓaɓaǁoʃa emikʰawulweni jaɓo ɓonake ɓaɓavutʰululela utʰuli lweziɲawo zaɓo ɓeza eikoniju aɓafundi ɓaɡǀ̤wala intokozo nomoja oŋǀ̤wele kwatʰi eikoniju ɓaŋena kaɲekaɲe esinaɡoɡeni laɓad͡ʒuda ɓakʰuluma kwaze kwakʰolwa isiǁuku esikʰulu saɓad͡ʒuda namaɡreki kepʰa aɓad͡ʒuda aɓaŋakʰolwaŋa ɓavusa aɓezizwe ɓaɓenza nɬizijombi ŋakuɓazalwane nokʰo ɓaɬala isikʰatʰi eside ɓefundisa ŋesiɓindi ŋeŋkosi ejafakazela izwi lomusa wajo iɓanika ukuɓa kwenziwe iziɓonakaliso nezimaŋaliso ŋezanɮa zaɓo kepʰa isiǁuku somuzi saɬukana pʰakatʰi aɓaɲe ɓaɓa ŋakuɓad͡ʒuda naɓaɲe ŋakuɓapʰostoli kwatʰi ukuɓa ɓasukelwe jisidumo saɓezizwe naɓad͡ʒuda kaɲe naɓaɓusi ɓaɓo sokuɓapʰatʰa kaɓi nokuɓakʰanda ŋamat͡ʃe ɓatʰi seɓekwazi lokʰo ɓaɓalekela emizini jaselikawonija ilistra nederɓe nasezweni laŋakʰona ɓaʃumajela kʰona ivaŋeli elistra kwakuɬezi indoda etʰile ejisilima ŋeziɲawo ejisiʃoʃa selokʰu jazalwa ŋunina eŋazaŋe ihambe jona jamuzwa upawulu ekʰuluma jena ejiɡǃ̤olozela waɓona ukutʰi inokukʰolwa kokuɓa ipʰiliswe watʰi ŋezwi elikʰulu sukuma ume ŋeziɲawo zakʰo jajisiɡǁ̤uma jahamba kwatʰike iziǁuku zikuɓona lokʰo akwenzile upawulu zapʰakamisa izwi lazo zatʰi ŋesilikawonija oŋkuluŋkulu ɓefana naɓantu ɓeɬele kitʰi uɓarnaɓa ɓambiza ŋokutʰi ud͡ʒupitʰeri upawulu ŋokutʰi umerkuriju ŋokuɓa kwakuŋuje owajehola ekukʰulumeni kepʰa umpristi kad͡ʒupitʰeri otʰempeli lakʰe lipʰambi komuzi waletʰa iziŋkunzi nemiɡeǁo jezimbali ŋasemasaŋweni wafuna ukuɓaɬaɓela ekaɲe neziǁuku kwatʰi ukuɓa ɓakuzwe lokʰo aɓapʰostoli oɓarnaɓa nopawulu ɓakxebula iziŋuɓo zaɓo ɓapʰonseka pʰakatʰi kwesiǁuku ɓememeza ɓetʰi madoda nikwenzelani lokʰu na natʰi siŋaɓantu aɓaɲd͡ʒeŋani ŋemvelo siniʃumajeza ivaŋeli ukuɓa nipʰenduke kulokʰo okujize nipʰendukele kuŋkuluŋkulu opʰilajo owenza izulu nomɬaɓa nolwanɮe nakʰo koŋke okukukʰo otʰe ŋezizukulwane eziɮulilejo wajeka izizwe zoŋke zihambe ŋezinɮela zazo nokʰo akajekaŋa ukuzifakazela ŋokwenza okuɬe waninika imvula jasezulwini nezikʰatʰi zenala eɡǀ̤walisa izinɬizijo zenu ŋokuɬe naŋokud͡ʒaɓula ɓekuʃo lokʰo ɓazijekisa kalukʰuni iziǁuku ukuɓa ziŋaɓaɬaɓeli kodwa kwafika aɓad͡ʒuda ɓevela eantijokija naseikoniju seɓezivumisile iziǁuku ɓamkʰanda upawulu ŋamat͡ʃe ɓamhudulela ŋapʰanɮe komuzi ɓetʰi usefile kepʰa kwatʰi aɓafundi ɓembuŋaɲele wavuka waŋena emzini ŋaŋomuso wamuka noɓarnaɓa ɓaja ederɓe seɓeliʃumajele ivaŋeli kulowo muzi ɓezuzile aɓafundi aɓaniŋi ɓaɓujela elistra naseikoniju naseantijokija ɓaǃinisa imipʰefumulo jaɓafundi ɓeɓaluleka ukuɓa ɓeme ekukʰolweni ɓetʰi simelwe ukuŋena embusweni kaŋkuluŋkulu ŋezinɬupʰeko eziniŋi seɓeɓakʰetʰele amaluŋa amaɓanɮa ŋamaɓanɮa ɓakʰuleka ɓezila ukuɮa ɓaɓanikela eŋkosini aseɓekʰolwa jijo ɓase ɓedaɓula ipʰisidija ɓaja epʰamfilija seɓekʰulumile izwi epʰerɡe ɓeɬela eatalija ɓasuka lapʰo ŋomkʰumbi ɓaja eantijokija lapʰo ɓaɓenikelwe kʰona emseni kaŋkuluŋkulu kulowo mseɓenzi aseɓewufezile kwatʰi ukuɓa ɓafike ɓaliɓutʰa iɓanɮa ɓalanda ŋakʰo koŋke uŋkuluŋkulu akwenzile ŋaɓo nokutʰi uvulele naɓezizwe isaŋo lokukʰolwa ɓase ɓeɬala naɓafundi isikʰatʰi esiŋesiŋǀane kweɬa aɓatʰile ed͡ʒudija ɓafundisa aɓazalwane ukutʰi uma niŋasokwa ŋomtʰetʰo kamose niŋesindiswe kutʰe ukuɓa kuvele ukupʰambana nokupʰikisana okukʰulu pʰakatʰi kwaɓo nopawulu noɓarnaɓa ɓaŋǃuma ukuɓa opawulu noɓarnaɓa naɓatʰile kuɓo ɓakʰupʰukele ed͡ʒerusalema kuɓapʰostoli namaluŋa ŋalejo ndaɓa ŋalokʰo ɓepʰelekezelwe jiɓanɮa ɓadaɓula ifenike nesamarija ɓalandisa ukupʰenduka kwaɓezizwe ɓenzela ɓoŋke aɓazalwane intokozo eŋkulu seɓefikile ed͡ʒerusalema ɓamukelwa jiɓanɮa naɓapʰostoli namaluŋa ɓakuɓika koŋke uŋkuluŋkulu aɓekwenzile ŋaɓo kepʰa kwasukuma aɓatʰile ɓeɬelo laɓafarisi aɓakʰolwajo ɓatʰi kumelwe ukuɓa ɓasokwe ɓajalwe ukuɡǀ̤ina umtʰetʰo kamose ɓase ɓeɓutʰana aɓapʰostoli namaluŋa ukuze ɓajiɬole lejo ndaɓa seɓepʰikisene kakʰulu wasukuma upetru watʰi kuɓo madoda ɓazalwane nijazi ukutʰi sekukade uŋkuluŋkulu wakʰetʰa pʰakatʰi kwenu ukuɓa aɓezizwe ɓezwe izwi levaŋeli ŋomlomo wami ɓakʰolwe uŋkuluŋkulu owazi inɬizijo waɓafakazela eɓapʰa umoja oŋǀ̤wele ɲd͡ʒeŋatʰi futʰi akaɬukanisaŋa ŋalutʰo pʰakatʰi kwetʰu naɓo eɬambulula izinɬizijo zaɓo ŋokukʰolwa maɲd͡ʒeke nimliŋelani uŋkuluŋkulu ŋokuɓeka id͡ʒoka entaɲeni jaɓafundi oɓaɓa natʰi esasiŋenamanɮa okulitʰwala na kepʰa sijakʰolwa ukutʰi sisindiswa ŋomusa weŋkosi ud͡ʒesu ŋanɮelaɲe naɓo isiǁuku soŋke satʰula ɓaɓelalela oɓarnaɓa nopawulu ɓelanda ŋeziɓonakaliso naŋezimaŋaliso zoŋke uŋkuluŋkulu aɓezenzile ŋaɓo pʰakatʰi kwaɓezizwe kepʰa seɓetʰulile ud͡ʒakoɓe watʰatʰa watʰi madoda ɓazalwane ŋilaleleni usimejoni uselandile ŋokuɬela kukaŋkuluŋkulu ekuǃaleni ukuɓa atʰatʰele iɡama lakʰe isizwe kuɓo aɓezizwe namazwi aɓaprofetʰi ajavumelana nalokʰo ɲd͡ʒeŋalokʰo kulot͡ʃiwe ukutʰi ‘emva kwalokʰo ŋijakuɓuja ŋijakʰe futʰi inɮu kadavide ewilejo ŋiɓuje ŋakʰe okudilikilejo kwajo ŋijimise ukuze aɓaselejo ɓaɓantu kaɲe naɓezizwe ɓoŋke ɓajifune iŋkosi eliɓizwe pʰezu kwaɓo iɡama lami iʃo iŋkosi ekwenza lokʰu okwaziwa kwapʰakade ŋakʰo mina ŋitʰi masiŋaɓakʰatʰazi laɓo kwaɓezizwe aɓapʰendukela kuŋkuluŋkulu kodwa masiɓaloɓele ukuɓa ɓajeke amaɲala ezitʰombe nawoɓufeɓe nawokuǃumbelenejo naweɡazi ŋokuɓa umose unaɓo aɓaʃumajelajo emizini joŋke kwasezizukulwaneni zasendulo efundwa emasinaɡoɡeni amasaɓatʰa ŋamasaɓatʰa kʰona kwaɓa kuɬe kuɓapʰostoli namaluŋa nakulo iɓanɮa loŋke ukutʰumela eantijokija nopawulu noɓarnaɓa amadoda akʰetʰiwejo pʰakatʰi kwaɓo ud͡ʒuda otʰiwa uɓarsaɓa nosila amadoda aŋaɓaholi pʰakatʰi kwaɓazalwane ɓaloɓa ŋesanɮa saɓo ŋokutʰi aɓapʰostoli namaluŋa aɓazalwane ɓajaɓiŋelela aɓazalwane aɓavela kwaɓezizwe aɓaseantijokija naɓasesirija naɓasekʰilikʰija ɲd͡ʒeŋalokʰo sizwile ukutʰi aɓaɲe aɓavela kitʰi ɓanikʰatʰazile ŋamazwi ɓeɲakazisa imipʰefumulo esiŋaɓajalelaŋa kʰona kwaɓa kuɬe kitʰi sesinɬizijoɲe ukutʰuma kini amadoda akʰetʰiwejo kaɲe naɓatʰandiwejo ɓetʰu oɓarnaɓa nopawulu aɓantu aɓadele ukupʰila kwaɓo ŋeŋǁa jeɡama leŋkosi jetʰu ud͡ʒesu kristu ŋalokʰo sitʰumile od͡ʒuda nosila aɓazakunit͡ʃela lezo zinto ŋomlomo ŋokuɓa kwaɓa kuɬe kumoja oŋǀ̤wele nakitʰi ukuɓa siŋanitʰwesi umtʰwalo omkʰulu ŋapʰanɮe kwalezi zinto ezifunekajo zokutʰi nijeke okuɬat͡ʃelwe izitʰombe neɡazi nokuǃumbelenejo noɓufeɓe uma nizilinda kulezo zinto noɓa nenza kaɬe salani kaɬe ŋakʰo seɓemukisiwe ɓeɬela eantijokija ɓaliɓutʰa iɓanɮa ɓalinika iŋǀwadi seɓejifundile ɓatʰokoza ŋenduduzo jajo od͡ʒuda nosila ɲd͡ʒeŋokuɓa naɓo ɓeŋaɓaprofetʰi ɓaɓaduduza aɓazalwane ŋamazwi amaniŋi ɓaɓaǃinisa seɓeɬale kʰona isikʰatʰi ɓamukiswa ŋaɓazalwane ŋokutʰula ɓaɓujela kuɓo aɓaɓatʰumilejo kepʰa kwaɓa kuɬe kusila ukuɓa asale kʰona kodwa opawulu noɓarnaɓa ɓaɬala eantijokija ɓefundisa ɓeʃumajela izwi leŋkosi kaɲe naɓaɲe aɓaniŋi emva kwezinsuku ezitʰile upawulu wajesetʰi kuɓarnaɓa ake siɓuje sihambele aɓazalwane emizini joŋke ŋamiɲe esaʃumajela kujo izwi leŋkosi siɓone ukutʰi ɓaɬezi kaɲd͡ʒani uɓarnaɓa waɬosa ukuhamba nod͡ʒohane otʰiwa umarku kepʰa upawulu watʰi akufanele ukuɓa ɓahambe naje owaɓaʃija epʰamfilija akaze aja naɓo emseɓenzini kwase kuvela ukupʰikisana okukʰulu ɓaze ɓaɬukana uɓarnaɓa watʰatʰa umarku wawelela ekʰupro ŋomkʰumbi kepʰa upawulu wazikʰetʰela usila wahamba enikelwe ŋaɓazalwane emseni weŋkosi wadaɓula isirija nekʰilikʰija eǃinisa amaɓanɮa kʰona weɬela ederɓe naselistra beka kwakukʰona lapʰo umfundi otʰile ŋutʰimotʰewu iɡama lakʰe indodana jowesifazane wakwad͡ʒuda okʰoliwejo kepʰa ujise wajeŋumɡreki owajefakazelwa kaɬe ŋaɓazalwane ɓaselistra naɓaseikoniju lowo upawulu watʰanda ukuɓa ahambe naje wamtʰatʰa wamsoka ŋeŋǁa jaɓad͡ʒuda aɓaɓekʰona kulezo zindawo ŋokuɓa ɓoŋke ɓaɓemazi ukutʰi ujise wajeŋumɡreki kwatʰi ɓedaɓula imizi ɓaɓanika iziŋǃumo ezaŋǃuɲwa ŋaɓapʰostoli namaluŋa ased͡ʒerusalema ukuɓa ɓaziɡǀ̤ine ɲd͡ʒaloke amaɓanɮa aǃiniswa ekukʰolweni anda ŋoɓuniŋi imiɬa ŋemiɬa ɓase ɓedaɓula izwe lasefriɡija nelaseɡalatʰija ɓeŋǃat͡ʃelwe ŋumoja oŋǀ̤wele ukulikʰuluma izwi easija seɓefikile ŋasemisija ɓaliŋa ukuja eɓitʰinija kepʰa umoja kad͡ʒesu akaɓavumelaŋa ɓaɮula emisija ɓeɬela etrowa kwaɓonakala kupawulu umbono eɓusuku indoda etʰile jasemakedonija ejajimi imŋǀeŋa jatʰi welela emakedonija usisize lapʰo esewuɓonile umbono safuna masiɲane ukuja emakedonija satʰi uŋkuluŋkulu usiɓizile ukuɓa siɓaʃumajeze ivaŋeli kʰona samuka etrowa ŋomkʰumbi saǃonda esamotrake ŋaŋomuso safika enejapʰoli sisuka lapʰo saja efilipi eliŋumuzi ojikʰanda lesifunda sasemakedonija ikoloni kulowo muzi saɬala izinsuku ezitʰile ŋosuku lwesaɓatʰa sapʰumela ŋapʰanɮe kwesaŋo ŋasemfuleni lapʰo satʰi ɓaɓevama ukukʰuleka kʰona saɬala pʰansi sakʰuluma kuɓo aɓesifazane aɓaɓeɓutʰene owesifazane otʰile oɡama lakʰe liŋulidija eŋumtʰeŋisi weziɓuɓende wasemzini wasetʰijatʰira okʰonza uŋkuluŋkulu walalela iŋkosi jajivula inɬizijo jakʰe ukuɓa aǃapʰele okwakʰuluɲwa ŋupawulu kutʰe esebapatʰiziwe kaɲe nenɮu jakʰe wasiŋǀeŋa watʰi uma nitʰi ŋikʰolekile eŋkosini ŋenani enɮini jami niɬale kʰona wasiǀindezela kwatʰi sija endaweni jokukʰuleka kwaɬaŋana natʰi intombazana enomoja woɓuŋoma ejajitʰolela aɓaninijo inzuzo eŋkulu ŋokubula jona jamlandela upawulu natʰi jamemeza jatʰi laɓa ɓantu ɓajiziŋǀeku zikaŋkuluŋkulu opʰezukoŋke ezimemezela kini inɮela jensindiso jakwenza lokʰo izinsuku eziniŋi kepʰa upawulu eseǀasukile wapʰenduka watʰi kumoja ŋijakujala eɡameni likad͡ʒesu kristu ukuɓa upʰume kujo wajesepʰuma ŋaso leso sikʰatʰi kwatʰi aɓaninijo seɓeɓonile ukutʰi itʰemba lenzuzo jaɓo limukile ɓaɓaɓamba opawulu nosila ɓaɓahudulela esiɡǀ̤awini pʰambi kwaɓaɓusi ɓaɓajisa ezinduneni ɓatʰi laɓa ɓantu ɓaɲakazisa umuzi wakitʰi ɓeŋaɓad͡ʒuda ɓafundisa imikʰuɓa esiŋavuɲelwe ukuɓa sijamukele sijenze tʰina esiŋamaroma isiǁuku sase siɓavukela nezinduna zajala ukuɓa ɓaɬut͡ʃulwe iziŋuɓo ɓaʃajwe ŋenduku seziɓaʃajile imivimbo eminiŋi zaɓapʰonsa etiloŋweni zajala umɡǀ̤iniziɓoʃwa ukuɓa aɓaɡǀ̤ine impela jena ejaliwe kaɲd͡ʒalo waɓapʰonsa etiloŋweni eliŋapʰakatʰi waɓopʰa iziɲawo zaɓo oɡoŋolweni kepʰa pʰakatʰi koɓusuku opawulu nosila ɓekʰuleka ɓamdumisa uŋkuluŋkulu ŋamahuɓo iziɓoʃwa zaɓezwa kwavela ŋokuzuma ukuzamazama komɬaɓa okukʰulu kwaze kwazaɲazaɲiswa izisekelo zetiloŋo kwavuleka kʰona lapʰo imiɲaŋo joŋke kwatʰukuluka neziɓopʰo zaɓo ɓoŋke kwatʰi umɡǀ̤iniziɓoʃwa epʰapʰama waɓona imiɲaŋo jetiloŋo ivulekile wajesehoʃa iŋkemba efuna ukuziɓulala ŋokuɓa watʰi iziɓoʃwa zipʰuɲukile kepʰa upawulu wamemeza ŋezwi elikʰulu watʰi uŋazilimazi ŋokuɓa sikʰona soŋke wajeseɓiza iziɓani waɡid͡ʒimela pʰakatʰi etʰutʰumela wawa pʰansi pʰambi kukapawulu nosila waɓakʰipʰela ŋapʰanɮe watʰi makʰosi ŋimelwe ukwenzani ukuɓa ŋisindiswe na ɓona ɓatʰi kʰolwa jiŋkosi ud͡ʒesu jikʰona uzakusindiswa wena nenɮu jakʰo ɓase ɓemʃumajeza izwi likaŋkuluŋkulu jena naɓo ɓoŋke aɓaɓesenɮini jakʰe waɓatʰatʰa ŋaso leso sikʰatʰi saseɓusuku waɓaɡeza imivimbo wabapatʰizwa kʰona lapʰo jena naɓo ɓoŋke aɓakʰe waɓeɲusela enɮini waɓaɓekela ukuɮa watʰokoza kaɲe nenɮu jakʰe joŋke ŋokukʰolwa ŋuŋkuluŋkulu kepʰa sekusile izinduna zatʰuma izikʰonzi zatʰi ɓakʰulule laɓo ɓantu umɡǀ̤iniziɓoʃwa waɓikela upawulu lawo mazwi watʰi izinduna zitʰumele ukuɓa nikʰululwe ŋakʰo pʰumani maɲd͡ʒe nihambe ŋokutʰula kepʰa upawulu watʰi kuzo ɓasiʃajile pʰambi kwaɓantu siŋalaɬwaŋa ǀala tʰina siŋaɓantu aɓaŋamaroma ɓasipʰonsa etiloŋweni maɲd͡ʒe ɓasikʰipʰa ŋasese na ǃʰaɓo akuze ɓona ɓasikʰipʰe izikʰonzi zaɓikela izinduna lawo mazwi zona zesaɓa sezizwa ukutʰi ɓaŋamaroma zeza zaɓaŋǀeŋa seziɓakʰipʰile zaɓaŋǁusa ukuɓa ɓamuke emzini ɓase ɓepʰuma etiloŋweni ɓaŋena kwalidija kwatʰi seɓeɓaɓonile aɓazalwane ɓaɓaduduza ɓamuka kwatʰi seɓedaɓulile iamfipʰoli neapʰolonija ɓafika etʰesalonika lapʰo kwakukʰona isinaɡoɡe laɓad͡ʒuda kepʰa upawulu ɲd͡ʒeŋokwenza kwakʰe waŋena kuɓo wapʰendulana naɓo amasaɓatʰa amatʰatʰu etʰatʰela emibalweni eɓavulela eɓaǀʰasisela ukutʰi kwakumelwe ukuɓa ukristu aɬupʰeke avuke kwaɓafilejo etʰi futʰi ud͡ʒesu lo eŋimʃumajela kini uŋukristu ɓase ɓevuma aɓaɲe kuɓo ɓaziɬaŋanisa nopawulu nosila futʰi nesiǁuku esikʰulu samaɡreki akʰolwajo kaɲe naɓesifazane aɓadumilejo aɓaŋejiŋǀ̤osana kepʰa aɓad͡ʒuda ɓenomhawu ɓatʰatʰa kumabukudwane aɓalisa aɓatʰile aɓaɓi ɓesusa isijalujalu pʰakatʰi kwaɓantu ɓaǁokozelisa umuzi ɓaɬasela inɮu kad͡ʒasoni ɓefuna ukuɓakʰipʰela kuɓantu kepʰa ɓeŋaɓafumani ɓamhudulela ud͡ʒasoni kaɲe naɓazalwane aɓatʰile kuɓapʰatʰimuzi ɓamemeza ɓatʰi laɓa aɓajaluzisa izwe loŋke seɓefikile nalapʰa ud͡ʒasoni uɓamukele ɓoŋke laɓa ɓenza okupʰambene nezimiso zikakesari ɓetʰi kukʰona eɲe iŋkosi ŋud͡ʒesu kepʰa ɓetʰusa isiǁuku naɓapʰatʰimuzi aɓezwa lokʰo ɓatʰatʰa isiɓambiso kud͡ʒasoni nakwaɓaɲe ɓaɓakʰulula kepʰa aɓazalwane ɓamukisa opawulu nosila masiɲane eɓusuku ukuɓa ɓaje eɓereja ɓona seɓefikile kʰona ɓaŋena esinaɡoɡeni laɓad͡ʒuda laɓoke ɓaɓeɓaɬe kunaɓasetʰesalonika ɓalamukela izwi ŋenɬizijo joŋke ɓaɬolisisa imibalo imiɬa ŋemiɬa ukuɓa ziɲd͡ʒalo jini lezo zinto ŋakʰo aɓaniŋi kuɓo ɓakʰolwa naɓesifazane aɓanesitʰunzi aɓaŋamaɡreki namadoda aŋejiŋǀ̤osana kwatʰi aɓad͡ʒuda ɓasetʰesalonika seɓezwile ukutʰi izwi likaŋkuluŋkulu limeɲezelwe ŋupawulu naseɓereja ɓeza nakʰona ɓaziɲakazisa ɓezivusa iziǁuku kʰona aɓazalwane ɓamukisa masiɲane upawulu ukuɓa aze afike elwanɮe kepʰa osila notʰimotʰewu ɓasala kʰona aɓampʰelekezelajo upawulu ɓamfikisa eatʰene kwatʰi seɓamukele isijalezo ŋosila naŋotʰimotʰewu sokuɓa ɓeze kuje ŋokuʃeʃa okukʰulu ɓamuka kwatʰi upawulu esaɓalinda eatʰene umoja wakʰe waǀunuka pʰakatʰi kwakʰe eɓona umuzi uɡǀ̤wele izitʰombe ŋakʰoke wakʰuluma esinaɡoɡeni kuɓad͡ʒuda nakuwo amakʰolwa nasesiɡǀ̤awini imiɬa ŋemiɬa kuɓo aɓaɓesuke ɓekʰona kepʰa aɓatʰile kuzo izazi zamaepikʰuru nezamastojiku ɓapʰikisana naje aɓaɲe ɓatʰi leli pʰoʃopʰoʃo litʰini na aɓaɲe ɓatʰi kuŋatʰi uŋomemezela oŋkuluŋkulu aɓaŋaziwajo ŋokuɓa wajeʃumajela ivaŋeli ŋod͡ʒesu naŋokuvuka kwaɓafilejo ɓase ɓemtʰatʰa ɓamjisa earejopʰaɡu ɓetʰi uŋesazise ukutʰi sijini lesi sifundiso esiʃa esikʰuluɲwa ŋuwe na ŋokuɓa uletʰa ezinɮeɓeni zetʰu okutʰile okuŋaziwajo ŋalokʰo sifuna ukwazi ukutʰi lokʰu kuŋaɓa jini
